It enjoys the natural beauty of "a city in a garden and a blend of city scenery"; it can be easily reached by car from the Beijing-Tibet Expressway and Jingli Expressway; next to the hotel is Wanda Plaza, which is only a short walk away It can be reached in 1 minute, and there is a food truck night market opposite, but it is lively. In terms of dining convenience alone, the Marriott Hotel has an advantage over the nearby Crowne Plaza and DoubleTree by Hilton!

Travel: Famous scenic spots are gathered in the surrounding area, including Badaling Great Wall, Longqing Gorge, Yeya Lake National Wetland Park, Expo Park, Shiyaju, and Baili Gallery. They are all within 10 minutes to an hour's drive from the hotel. If you plan a two-day trip to Yanqing, it is suitable to choose to stay here!

Dining: The hotel has a Chinese restaurant, which can be ordered a la carte or buffet. It is delicious and affordable; there is an executive lounge on the 11th floor, which provides afternoon tea and happy hour for privileged guests. The breakfast is rich, beautifully styled, and tastes authentic, such as pancakes, cheese, croissants, etc., everything is good. The coffee can be packed and comes with an anti-scalding mat, which is considerate! One thing worth mentioning is that although the rooms are full on weekends, due to the diligent and capable staff and proper hotel management, there are no crowds or crowds at any time and in any place. The breakfast room is very orderly, thumbs up!

Facilities: The hotel has 12 floors. The density is not high. The decoration is simple and elegant, modern and exquisite. The room layout is reasonable, the sofa is large in size, the bedding is comfortable, and the mountains can be seen outside the window, and the scenery is pleasant.

Other facilities: There are children's rooms, gyms and swimming pools, clean, bright and tidy!

Service: This is the most noteworthy point. Every staff member is lovely and polite, especially the beautiful lady at the front desk, who provided considerate service for our family's stay. Before traveling, she introduced the basic situation of the hotel to us in detail and recommended nearby attractions; during check-in, she quickly checked in for us and kept a smile on her face at all times, which reflected the professionalism of Marriott employees; after check-in, she They are also always available to answer our various questions and follow up on our stay experience. The above fully reflects Marriott Hotel‚Äôs guest-first service concept and impressive soft power. I would like to express my gratitude to all the hotel staff and Xiao Jiang~

This is definitely a place you should visit. I still want to come here and will come again in the future. I recommend Yanqing five-star resort hotel to everyone!
